theorem P14 {a b c : ℝ} (ha : a > 0) (hb : b > 0) (hc : c > 0) (h : a * b * c = 1) : 1 / 3 ≤ (1 / (a ^ 5 * (b + 2 * c) ^ 2)) + (1 / (b ^ 5 * (c + 2 * a) ^ 2)) + (1 / (c ^ 5 * (a + 2 * b) ^ 2)) := by  
  make_homogeneous 1 / 3 - ((a * b * c) ^ (7 / 3) / (((2 * a + c) ^ 2) * (b ^ 5))) - ((a * b * c) ^ (7 / 3) / (((a + 2 * b) ^ 2) * (c ^ 5))) - ((a * b * c) ^ (7 / 3) / (((b + 2 * c) ^ 2) * (a ^ 5))) ≤ 0
  scale Holder_2R_pq_div_variant1_right_3vars (u1 := 1) (u2 := 1) (u3 := 1) (v1 := (b + (2 * c))) (v2 := (a + (2 * b))) (v3 := ((2 * a) + c)) (w1 := a) (w2 := c) (w3 := b) (p := 2) (q := 5) (k := (((a * b) * c) ^ (7 / 3))) (l := 0) (left := 1 / 3)
  llm_simplify 1 / 3 - ((a * b * c) ^ (7 / 3) * (((1 / a ^ 3) ^ (1 / 3) + (1 / c ^ 3) ^ (1 / 3) + (1 / b ^ 3) ^ (1 / 3)) ^ 3 / ((b + 2 * c) * a + (a + 2 * b) * c + (2 * a + c) * b) ^ 2)) = 1 / 3 - ((a * b + a * c + b * c) ^ 3 / (((3 * a * b + 3 * a * c + 3 * b * c) ^ 2) * (a ^ (2 / 3)) * (b ^ (2 / 3)) * (c ^ (2 / 3))))
  llm_cancel_factor (1 / 3) - ((a * b + a * c + b * c) ^ 3 / ((3 * a * b + 3 * a * c + 3 * b * c) ^ 2 * a ^ (2 / 3) * b ^ (2 / 3) * c ^ (2 / 3))) = (1 / 9) * (1 / (a ^ (2 / 3))) * (1 / (b ^ (2 / 3))) * (1 / (c ^ (2 / 3))) * (3 * a ^ (2 / 3) * b ^ (2 / 3) * c ^ (2 / 3) - (a * b) - (a * c) - (b * c))
  scale AM_GM_normal_right_3vars (u := (b * c)) (v := (a * c)) (w := (a * b)) (k := 1) (l := 0) (left := 3 * a ^ (2 / 3) * b ^ (2 / 3) * c ^ (2 / 3))
  sym_simplify 3 * a ^ (2 / 3) * b ^ (2 / 3) * c ^ (2 / 3)  -  3 * (b * c * a * c * a * b) ^ (1 / 3) = 0
